HTTP is the protocol for the old world, the server-client based cloud paradigm.
By moving away from HTTP and authoring everything in a Bitcoin native way (using Bitcoin transaction ids and content hashes) we can build a completely self-contained network of documents which can exist forever on the blockchain. -un
